# Excalidraw Data
## Text Elements
The current will be zero inside the body because the penetration of the magnetic field will be only a few microns. If the magnet is moved much slower, then the response from the electrons will start reaching their collision times and the field will penetrate further and further into the body, starting to induce currents within the body. If it moves so fast that the electrons on the surface move faster than their collision times, then only the electrons at the surface are required to move in order to cancel out the field, the inner electrons are thereby shielded. The surface electron movement exactly cancels out the incoming field, meaning that the electrons moving don't have residual fields that can effect the inner electrons because the addition of the two fields is exactly zero. (The magnet has to move fast enough to overcome the collision time of the electrons.) ^AK67BNvb
